Brought our puppy there for their puppy social. He developed kennel cough from Klub K9. Since puppies don't have all their shots, we thought that Klub K9 would be a safe place where he wouldn't get sick....WRONG!! After this, I heard Klub K9 was shut down previously due to dog flu.< /review>

< resp>
{'time': 1561677141429, 'text': 'Sorry to hear that your puppy got kennel cough. For the puppy social event, we will deep clean the area one night before and lock it down until the puppy social starts. We also require the puppy owners not to bring their puppy to dog parks or the other puppy socials to try to avoid fleas or the other virus such as kennel cough. Unfortunately not every owner listens to us.\n\nYes, I deiced to shut down for Canine Influenza H3N2 in January of 2018. The influenza hit California in December of 2017. Before  that it had never been in California. Prior to the outbreak veterinarians did not carry the vaccine for the H2N3 influenza. Due to the fact that it had never been to California.\n\nDuring the Christmas holiday we close daycare due to high volume of overnight boarding dogs. During this time we had no cases of any kind of sickness including influenza. Shortly after the holiday we opened back up for daycare dogs. We had a dog enter for daycare who was in the beginning stages of the flu. According to our vet a dog will be infected and contagious for typically 7 days prior to showing any symptoms of influenza. Unfortunately high tech glasses that make germs visible to the human eye have not been invented yet. Through the process of elimination we determined which dog was the original dog who brought it into our facility. The owner confessed he had been taking him to a dog park to burn off energy while our daycare was closed. And we can\'t blame him dogs need exercise, and he certainly couldn\'t see any germs on his dog either. The same goes for our puppy social. We try our best to make sure everyone is up to date with vaccines, but its really up to the owner and their veterinarian to make sure they are protected.\n\nLet me be clear we where never "shut down" by anyone, I chose to close. The reason I deiced to shut down was try to break the infection chain. I think it was clearly a better option, rather than  staying opening and getting more dogs sick. The two weeks I shut down caused me to directly lose $90,000, but I believe it\'s worth to keep dogs safe.\n\nWe try to be as safe as possible here. Personally my vet vaccinated all my puppies at 8 weeks for Distemper, parvovirus and bordetella aka kennel cough. I would imagine any vet you talk to about joining a puppy social would strongly recommend getting bordetella prior to attending, as that vaccine covers the most common strains of kennel cough. However unfortunately less common strains do exist that are not covered by the bordetella vaccine. And lets face it no vaccine is perfect. People who get flu shots occasionally get the flu.\n\nWe have a very stringent cleaning process here to ensure people have a clean, safe and fun place for their puppies to come and socialize and burn off energy while learning basic social skills. We urge all owners to discuss vaccines and when to get them with their veterinarian. We highly recommend having Distemper, parvovirus and bordetella prior to joining any kind or canine gathering or social to help keep them safe.\nThanks,\nKlub K9'}</resp>

I'm going to give those guys 5stars. I bought two full kitchens from them over the years and have two more coming. Yes the service may not be perfect, it's a warehouse but you get what you pay for. If you can point me to the place that has better selection and quality with at least the same pricing, i will be glad to check. I had no issues with granit and onyx slabs and at times i picked up when purchased and a few times i marked the items i liked and picked up later. I picked up kitchen cabinets assembled and boxed whenever it was convenient for me. They may be understuffed at times and you may need to wait a bit longer than some place but if you expect a boutique experience just don't go there and bash the place. It's not a botique store and it never meant to be. It may not have everything in there nut it has enough of selection to satisfy many different tastes when it comes to materials. As far as kitchen cabinets they only have like 5 choices, so it is very simple, you either like it or not. The bottom line is you get a great deal for what you get. If you are not ready to deal with some minor hassle to work through it, get a contractor and let them do the job for you. But in that case they will not pick the right color or will not get something on time, right? Life happens, things don't always go as expected or scheduled in a remodel or construction in general, just accept it ;) there are things you can't change.

I will by from those guys again. That being said, i didn't use their install it cutting services, so can't comment on that side.< /Review>

< review>
I feel that the ball was completely dropped when it came to the production of our wedding. This is a day that we can't do over or get back and we feel that most of our issues were directly due to the service or lack there of that we received. I expressed concern about keeping our timeline during the details meeting and was told by Kimberly that a point person would be present to keep the event on schedule and lias between the venue and us.

Carlos was present to assist us in the bridal suite and aside from not having a direct contact for him, he was great and promptly assisted with our needs. When I met the point person she did not identify her self as such. I assumed she was apart of the kitchen staff because we only discussed when the food would be set up and served. I'm not sure if she failed to do her job or if I was misinformed by Kimberly on the tasks that a point person would be responsible for. There was no one to keep us on time or to help us line up for the ceremony which led to me standing in the hallway speaking with the bartender and "point person" about the bar and dinner times as I waited to walk down the aisle in the middle of my ceremony.

When our initial $500 ran out at the bar guests were charged for drinks instead of our "point person" informing us. Less than half of our expected 96 guests were in attendance so as I was told by Elizabeth, the policy was that the money from those guests be reallocated to the bar. Unfortunately, when this issue was brought up to me I explained that to the point person and was told that I needed to wait for the manager to arrive. When he arrived an hour later our request was put into place and he did offer an additional $100 towards the bar which we appreciated but I was upset that if we had not discussed it that the Grand intended to profit from our ignorance.

Later in the evening I noticed that the food stations were empty and food was no longer being served so I assumed that we had finished everything but that seemed odd since we had less guests than we had planned for. Resulting in our mothers, the groom and probably guests as well not getting a chance to eat. At the end of the night the remaining food was wheeled out and given to us which made us wonder why we were not informed that they would be closing down so that we could announce it to guests instead of the event ending and wasting the food we had purchased. Overall we do not feel that this was worth the almost $6000 spent. I cried several times through out my wedding day and none were happy tears. We are so extremely disappointed which is a complete 180 from how we felt when we found this venue. We were promptly contacted about any and all payments due but that same urgency and concern was not taken when it came to our event. And on top of that I felt pressured to add even more guests to our final count since I was told by Kimberly that even though I purchased the tables that the Grand could not provide another table without additional guests. Which resulted in us paying even more money than we intended and not allowing us to properly account for no shows.

Overall I wish that we would have went with a different venue because here we definitely got less than what we paid for.< /review>
